Current Commentary

The Question of Solidarity in the World of Opinion

— Star

Organized public opinion is the driving force of democratic politics and the main condition for victory in diplomacy and military affairs. For public opinion to be organized and powerful, the world of opinion, which bears the responsibility of leading and expressing it, must first have a sound organization, strong unity, and close cooperation. China is currently in a time that most requires sound public opinion, yet it has not demonstrated the necessary strength. The biggest difficulty is the inability of the world of opinion to unite. Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Journalists Association held a general meeting, and some advocated inviting all registered newspaper reporters to join the association as members in order to improve the organization of the journalists' association. This suggestion is worthy of consideration by the world of opinion.

News reporters, whose profession it is to lead society and represent the people, should at least have the professional status of lawyers, doctors, and teachers in order to ensure the sanctity and honor of their profession. We cannot deny that the procedures for entering the profession of journalism are sometimes too lax. After becoming a reporter, the degree of supervision by colleagues is also insufficient. In European and American countries, there are few that do not have sound journalists' organizations. The task of these organizations is to raise professional standards, improve the lives of reporters, jointly study the knowledge and skills that reporters should possess, and represent the entire world of opinion in contact with all sectors. Of course, European and American journalists' organizations include British and American press organizations that are purely journalist-centric, as well as German and Italian journalists' organizations that take national interests as their highest principle. Although both types of organizations have their critics, from the perspective of the press and the entire society and country, having these organizations is an improvement over the era of laissez-faire.

Even in Germany, where freedom of speech is most restricted, the German Journalists' Association, according to the 1933 German Journalists' Law, has the responsibility to monitor all members' fulfillment of their obligations and to protect their rights. Anyone who is not a member of the German Journalists' Association cannot practice journalism in Germany. The Central Journalists' Association seeks to cultivate journalistic talent and promote the common welfare of the press. All disputes in the press are handled by the professional court attached to the association. We cannot arbitrarily assume that this organization is a tool for Hitler to suppress freedom of speech, because Germany already had this professional organization before Hitler came to power. The high achievements of the German press in terms of quality are mostly due to the sound journalists' organization. In the United Kingdom, the United States, and other countries, journalists' national bodies not only seek to improve their lives and raise their status, but also study the improvement of the newspaper industry and seek common propositions and views on certain issues.

In extraordinary times, the preparation for the mobilization of opinion is even more important than military and economic mobilization. Because without public opinion and morale, nothing can be pushed forward. The press bears the greatest responsibility to the country. However, the press today has not yet achieved the same strict organization as the military, or the same level of cooperation and unity as the transportation industry. Therefore, a sound organization is an urgent requirement for actively improving the newspaper industry, promoting public spirit, and passively coping with the extraordinary situation and clarifying the press. This is what the press needs, and it is also what the 400 million people of China, whom they represent, need most.

Closing Day of the Pan-American Conference: U.S. Secretary of State Announces New Monroe Doctrine: The Americas Unite to Defend Against External Aggression, Setting a Peaceful Example for the World

"Either Eliminate War, or Be Eliminated by War"

(Buenos Aires) At the closing of the Pan-American Peace Conference in the capital of Argentina today, U.S. Secretary of State Hull delivered an inspiring speech, stating, in brief, that we must eliminate war, or war will eliminate us. Now that a list has been made for each country to examine its own goals and government, each country should, like an individual, forgive and forget the damages inflicted by other countries. He must solemnly declare that the American countries are not moving towards an isolationist policy. The American countries will never harbor the illusion of egoism, knowing the harm of this doctrine. In this closely organized and interdependent world, we deeply feel the folly of building a Great Wall of China around the New Hemisphere. Our purpose is not to isolate the American continent, but to delineate the path by which we can achieve peace, thereby setting an effective example for other parts of the world. Free people of the world do not believe that war is inevitable. They are no longer intimidated by the spears of warmongers. They will loudly stop those who seek to destroy peace for the sake of power. They believe that the future peace can be guaranteed by the development of public opinion everywhere, because that public opinion will completely condemn the actions of politicians who promote militarism, etc. (Reuters, 23rd)

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull recently delivered a closing address to the Inter-American Conference, praising the conference's ability to unite the American nations to resist external aggression. Responsible parties here believe that this is the New Monroe Doctrine announced by the United States. Informed observers stated that such an interpretation will implicitly transform the Monroe Doctrine from a policy of the United States alone into a common policy of all American countries. Therefore, the American nations will henceforth jointly bear the responsibility of maintaining peace in the Americas and resisting external aggression. If the nations of Europe and Asia dare to attack the Americas, the combined forces of the navies and armies of all American nations will respond, not just the military strength of the United States alone. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Chairman's Address

The Pan-American Peace Conference in the capital of Argentina, which began on the first of this month, has lasted more than twenty days. The closing ceremony was held today, with the chairman, Argentine Foreign Minister Lamas, delivering an address, stating that this conference has benefited both the Americas and world peace, and is worthy of attention. The results are numerous, and the most important are (1) the method of consultation, that is, the American countries should consult each other to prevent or stop wars through joint and concerted action; (2) the principle of non-intervention, that is, other countries should not interfere in the internal affairs and foreign affairs of each country that do not involve other countries. "According to the Geneva Protocol of 1924, all countries should enjoy equal sovereignty and have the right to pursue a policy of neutrality. We now reiterate this and seek new ways to achieve neutrality in order to avoid the scourge of war. The 'Declaration of Cooperation among American Countries' is sufficient to prove the existence of democratic rule and joint responsibility, and reiterates that all wars of aggression and violent intervention are illegal... In short, if disputes occur between the American countries in the future, they must be resolved by peaceful means. Even when wars occur outside the Americas, we should cooperate with other countries to stop the conflict, because although we pursue a policy of neutrality, we cannot ignore the scourge of war," etc. (Havas, 24th)

Philippine Islands Issue: Consultation Principle Applies

(Washington) At the closing of the Pan-American Peace Conference today, representatives from 21 countries placed great emphasis on the principle of mutual consultation. This has raised speculation among U.S. authorities as to whether this principle can also be implemented in the Pacific in the future. It is said that the conversation between U.S. High Commissioner to the Philippines Murphy and President Roosevelt next Monday, and Philippine President Quezon's planned trip to the United States in February or March of next year, may indicate that the government is trying to implement the neutrality of the Philippines. Therefore, the government may consult with countries related to the Pacific. (Note: Article 11 of the Philippine Independence Act stipulates that the President should negotiate with other countries as soon as possible to recognize the permanent neutrality of the Philippines after its independence.) Observers believe that no matter how the Philippine issue is resolved, this consultation plan can enhance the U.S. position, that is, the Pacific issue should be resolved through mutual consultation among all interested countries, rather than through any bilateral agreement. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Japan Plans to Suggest to the U.S. Negotiations on Pacific Issues

(Washington) It is reported that Japanese Foreign Minister Arita plans to propose to the United States to conduct negotiations on the issue of Japanese-American relations in the Pacific. Semi-official circles here have expressed considerable goodwill towards this news, believing that according to the Philippine Independence Act, the island will separate from the United States and become independent in 1946. The United States should try to guarantee the neutral status of the Philippines before that date. If Japan is willing to start negotiations with the United States now, it will be easier for the United States to guarantee the neutral status of the Philippines. (Havas, 23rd)

18th Session of the League of Nations Assembly to Be Convened at the End of January Next Year, Abyssinia to Lose Right to Attend

(Geneva) The 18th session of the League of Nations Assembly will be convened between January 25th and February 5th of next year to vote on Egypt's admission as a member state. League of Nations officials recently announced that notices of the assembly meeting will be sent to all member states at the end of this month. The Administrative Council originally planned to meet on January 18th of next year, but it may have to be postponed by several days due to the simultaneous holding of the assembly. In addition, the United Kingdom and France will submit a proposal to all member states of the League of Nations, asking them not to allow the Abyssinian delegation to attend the League of Nations again, so that the factual status of the country can be determined, and Italy can cooperate with the League of Nations again. (Havas, 24th)

Drafts of Two International Conventions: China's Reply Sent to the League of Nations, Expressing Acceptance of the Establishment of an International Criminal Court, Two Suggestions Made for Punishing Terrorism

(Geneva) Regarding the issue of punishing international terrorism, the League of Nations Administrative Council's Committee of Legal Experts previously drafted two types of conventions, one being the Convention for the Suppression and Prevention of Terrorism, and the other being the Convention for the Establishment of an International Criminal Court. The Administrative Council sent them to the governments of all member states for review. The Chinese government recently sent a reply to League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, accepting in principle the proposal to establish an International Criminal Court. Regarding the issue of suppressing and preventing terrorism, it stated that it was regrettable that the Committee of Legal Experts had failed to consider the proposal submitted by the Chinese government. The Chinese government felt that it was difficult to punish terrorism due to the existence of concessions, public concessions, and leased territories in China, and requested that the Committee of Legal Experts study it again. According to the Chinese government's proposal, there were two items: (1) Any country that enjoys extraterritoriality in another country should have consular courts to manage cases involving its nationals. If such nationals commit crimes of political terrorism, they should be transferred to the jurisdiction of the judicial authorities of the host country. (2) Any country that administers part of the administrative affairs in another country due to the existence of concessions, public concessions, and leased territories within the territory of another country should provide all kinds of conveniences to the judicial authorities of the host country when punishing political terrorism. (Havas, 24th)

Japanese Parliament Convenes and Establishes, Opening Ceremony to Be Held Tomorrow

(Tokyo) The 70th Ordinary Session of the Japanese Parliament convened at 9:00 AM on the 24th in the newly completed Parliament Building. All members of the House of Peers and the House of Representatives attended. After determining the seats of each member, each department elected its ministers, directors, etc. Thereupon, the parliament was established. (Domei, 24th)

(Tokyo) The opening ceremony of the Japanese Parliament is scheduled to be held at 11:00 AM on the 26th in the House of Peers. The Emperor is scheduled to personally attend the venue that morning, bestow a rescript, and then return to the palace. (Domei, 24th)

(Tokyo) In view of the fact that diplomatic issues are valued by all factions, at the factional negotiation meeting on the 24th, some people advocated that Daikichi Tagawa from the Second Lounge should raise an urgent question on diplomatic issues on the 27th. The negotiation meeting did not approve, and it was shelved. Although both the Seiyukai and Minseito parties are concerned about diplomatic issues to a considerable extent, they do not have the enthusiasm to raise them as a formal agenda item and decide on the party's attitude. Even if the government's beliefs are questioned by other means, diplomatic issues will not be questioned in the form of urgent questions before the parliamentary recess. (Domei, 24th)

Cuban President Recently Removed from Office, Issues Address to the Nation, Worrying About the Future of the Political Situation

Havana: The special court formed by the Senate tonight tried the President's impeachment, and with a vote of 22 to 12, ruled that President Gómez should be removed from office immediately and replaced by Vice President Laredo Brú in accordance with the constitution (scheduled to be sworn in at noon tomorrow). As for most of the cabinet members, they have now resigned en masse. Earlier, Senator Portela had presented and read the defense statement personally drafted by the President, stating in brief: "This impeachment case is a violation of the constitution. Its motive is not to uphold justice and fairness, but to force me to resign. I am willing to abide by all rulings of the special court, but I must appeal to public opinion to clarify right and wrong. After I leave office, an era of infighting for power and profit will begin in the country. The freedom and rights of the Cuban people will also disappear completely. Democratic politics will come to an end from then on, and a dictatorship will rise up." (Havas, 23rd)

Havana: President Gómez recently issued an address to the nation from his private residence, attacking Colonel Batista, the Chief of Staff of the Army, with all his might, stating in brief: "Does Colonel Batista dare to openly establish a dictatorship? All he has done is reactionary. I am a Cuban revolutionary and should criticize him. We have suffered greatly from tyranny and have risen up to resist since former President Machado fled." Finally, the President wished the people of the country a safe Christmas. (Havas, 24th)

Havana: The President's dispute with the Parliament and Army leader Colonel Batista this time was over the sugar tax of nine cents, which was used to establish rural schools for the army. It has been passed by both houses, but the President believes that such schools will turn Cuban youth into warlords, which led to Batista's attack on the President, saying that if the people want a dictatorship, he can be a dictator. Now that the President has resigned, a military coup is unlikely to occur. (National Telegram, 23rd)

(Washington) The sudden surge in Cuban national politics, with President Gómez having been removed from office by a special court, has all been noted by the U.S. State Department. Some even asked whether the new government to be established in Cuba is in accordance with the law. (Havas, 23rd)

Professor of Peking Medical University Discovers Ancient Human Bones, Dating Back 500,000 Years

(Tokyo) "Sinanthropus pekinensis" is the oldest Neanderthal bone in Europe, discovered near Beijing in 1929. It is considered to be the oldest human bone in the world, along with the so-called Java Man, which was discovered in Java 40 years ago. However, in the middle of last month, Professor Hua Ding of Peking Medical University also discovered similar human bones in Yanjiaodian, east of Beijing, which has attracted attention from the archaeological community. The new discoveries include four skull bones, twelve skull fragments and lower jaw bones, and hundreds of teeth, belonging to two adult corpses. The human bones are almost in the same location as those discovered in 1929, buried only ten feet deep in the soil. These human bones are believed to be 500,000 years old. It is said that cannibals at the time hid in caves to avoid diseases. Peking Medical University was greatly stimulated by this discovery and will continue to excavate after receiving support from the American oil tycoon. (Domei, 24th)

Pope Reads Encyclical, Calls for World Peace, Criticizes Red Propaganda Movement, and Attacks German Heresy

Vatican City: At 11:30 this morning (7:30 PM Shanghai time), the Pope delivered a speech from his sickbed using a specially made silver-plated microphone, appealing for peace to the world. After the Pope finished his speech, it was immediately translated into English. The entire speech was probably quite lengthy. Because the Pope had just recovered from a long illness, his doctor, Dr. Milani, would be at his side to administer medicine at any time. (Reuters, 24th)

Vatican City: Pope Pius XI recently used a radio broadcast to read the Christmas encyclical. He began by saying that the current crisis was urgent and that the whole world and the Catholic Church were under threat. He specifically mentioned the Spanish Civil War at length, saying that "the civil war is intensifying, with mutual killings and destruction reaching extreme cruelty." He then denounced the communist propaganda movement and attacked German heresy. Finally, he prayed for peace, saying that while appealing to the whole world, we should still sincerely pray to God to obtain peace and tranquility, and that justice should be realized between individuals and groups, because only by achieving peace can we enjoy peace, and without justice, order cannot be maintained. (Havas, 24th)

Hitler Goes to Villa to Spend Christmas, Discusses Current Situation with Aides Before Leaving Capital

(Berlin) German leader Hitler left for the Berghof villa in Berchtesgaden last night, planning to stay there until January 11th of next year, so all official duties were suspended, and preparations were made for the holiday. After Hitler left Berlin, the worries about imminent conflicts in Europe were relieved. It was originally scheduled for Hitler to go to the villa on Tuesday, but he did not leave that day. Instead, he spent the whole day meeting with Aviation Minister General Göring, Defense Minister General von Blomberg, and other important officials. For a time, rumors spread, and people generally believed that the meeting was about the overall situation in Spain, the implementation of the non-intervention agreement, and economic issues. It is said that Hitler instructed his subordinates not to give him Christmas gifts, but Hitler himself sent several of his adjutants to buy suitable Christmas gifts several weeks ago so that they could be distributed to his friends and colleagues under the Christmas tree in Hitler's villa tonight amidst songs. (Reuters, 24th)

U.S. Celebrates Christmas, Full of Prosperity, Post Offices Are Extremely Busy, Stores Triple Their Profits

(New York) The prosperity of this year's Christmas in the United States is unprecedented in many years. The number of letters at the national postal offices is truly rare. The offices originally had 20,000 employees, but because the workload was too busy, 5,000 temporary office workers were hired. Several overdue European mail ships will arrive in New York tonight or tomorrow, carrying a total of 27,000 mailbags. The postal office will try its best to deliver them before the 25th. Transportation by national aviation, railways, and highways is also extremely congested. Many New York residents braved the cold and flocked to major stores to buy goods, so each store more than tripled its profits. Social events are gradually returning to the state before the recession. (Reuters, 23rd)

Intervention in the Spanish Civil War Intensifies in Germany, Number of Volunteers Entering Western Territory Increases, Several Foreign Warships Participate in Blockade of Ports

(London) According to informed sources, Italians have been gradually withdrawing from the territory controlled by the Spanish rebels, while Germans are continuously entering the country, and their numbers are increasing. For example, 9,000 Germans arrived in Cadiz, a port controlled by the Nationalists, on November 21st, another 600 arrived on November 26th, and on December 6th, six Junkers aircraft made in Germany were transported to the port, all equipped with 42-millimeter cannons. It is also said that several foreign warships have changed to the flags of the Spanish Nationalists and participated in the blockade of the port of Barcelona. For example, the Nationalist army has a cruiser, the "Admiral Cervera," participating in the blockade, but some people have glimpsed the ship at three different places at the same time, indicating that at least two ships are disguised as foreign warships and using the name of the ship. In addition, according to reports from informed sources, Barcelona, Valencia, and Madrid are all controlled by anarchists. The Soviet authorities only cooperate with the anarchists and have no contact with the Spanish Communist Party, because the Communist Party in Spain is small in number and its influence is not great. In the territory controlled by the Republican government, there are occasional cases of people going out at night to kill anti-government elements, but these are all irresponsible individual actions. As for the Republican government authorities, they have done their utmost to prohibit terrorist actions. According to general observers, the people of Spain are deeply tired of foreign intervention in the civil war, so mediation of the civil war may be possible in the near future. (Havas, 23rd)

Adjustment Committee Passes Detailed Monitoring Plan, Awaiting Agreement from Relevant Governments, Then Submitted to Warring Parties with Deadline for Reply

(London) The Non-Intervention in the Spanish Civil War Adjustment Committee met at the Foreign Office here today for two hours and unanimously passed a detailed plan to monitor the shipment of arms to Spain by sea, land, and air. Relevant governments are required to reply by January 1st of next year. If all countries agree, the plan will be submitted to the warring parties in Spain with a deadline of ten days to endorse it. Today's meeting also resolved to ask relevant countries to submit documents to the committee by January 4th of next year, stating whether they are prepared to allocate funds to implement the aforementioned plan, and the percentage of their contribution has been explained to them by the committee. (Reuters, 23rd)

(London) The government has recently decided to instruct the ambassadors stationed in Germany, Italy, and Russia, and the minister stationed in Portugal, to explain repeatedly to the governments of their respective host countries that the non-intervention measures in the Spanish Civil War must be monitored, and it is also necessary to prohibit foreign volunteers from going to Spain to participate in the civil war. Responsible parties believe that the influx of volunteers from certain countries to Spain will inevitably cause serious repercussions and will greatly hinder the prospects for peace in Europe. (Havas, 23rd)

France Expresses Strict Neutrality; Will Change Current Policy if Other Countries Don't Cease Interference

(London) The Times recently published a dispatch from its Paris correspondent stating that the French government has issued a public announcement. It states that if the involved countries do not adopt the proposals of the Non-Intervention Committee on the Spanish conflict to ensure that the non-intervention agreement can be effectively implemented, the French government will change its current policy. This action is due to the increasing interference of Germany in the Spanish Civil War and not due to the communist propaganda movement in that country. (24th Havas Dispatch)

(London) Lord Plymouth, Chairman of the Non-Intervention Committee on the Spanish Conflict and Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs, recently inquired of the governments of the involved countries about their opinions on prohibiting indirect intervention in the Spanish Civil War. (Note: "Indirect intervention" refers to the dispatch of volunteers from various countries to serve in Spain and the provision of financial assistance to both sides of the civil war.) Regarding this issue, the French government sent a reply to Plymouth today. According to responsible sources, the French government, in its reply, listed the various measures it is currently taking and expressed its willingness to adopt legislative procedures to prohibit indirect intervention in the Spanish conflict. However, France will only do so after other countries have also adopted similar legislative decisions. It is also said that the French government intends to crack down on both French and foreign nationals traveling to Spain, and all those wishing to travel to Spain must be investigated to ensure that they have legitimate reasons before passports are issued. In addition, the French government also intends to take other measures to prohibit the provision of financial assistance to both sides of the Spanish Civil War. (23rd Havas Dispatch)

Britain Feels Uneasy About Germany's Actions in Spain; Hopes Germany Will Change its Attitude and Ease Tensions

(London) Germany's economic situation is extremely dire, especially the food supply. It is rumored that the authorities are now planning to ration food. Upon hearing this news, political and economic figures here are extremely uneasy, fearing that if this situation worsens, Germany's interference in the Spanish Civil War may intensify in order to find a way out. The London stock market has already been affected by this. Although responsible figures in London still hope that the work currently being carried out by the Non-Intervention Committee on the Spanish Conflict will reduce German interference and thereby avoid a major disaster. In addition, regarding Germany's proposal to restore colonies, responsible figures in the UK believe that some of these colonies are administered by the UK under the mandate of the League of Nations, and their transfer of jurisdiction is not something that the British government can decide. Regarding the issue of raw material redistribution, its solution is actually part of the overall solution to various European problems, and only then can the UK consider it. (23rd Havas Dispatch)

(London) German Ambassador Ribbentrop returned to his country some days ago to spend Christmas. Political figures here very much hope that when the ambassador returns to his post, he will bring new instructions from his government on the issues of prohibiting volunteers from joining the Spanish Civil War and the future Locarno Treaty, so that the international situation can be eased. Responsible figures say that the British government is currently conducting negotiations with various governments, especially the German government, through diplomatic channels, requesting the prohibition of volunteers from joining the Spanish Civil War, and declaring that this move is necessary to maintain peace in Europe. Regarding this, Ambassador Ribbentrop had discussed it with Foreign Secretary Eden before returning to his country. Foreign Secretary Eden said at the time that Britain is eager to resolve general European problems, but as far as is generally known, the biggest obstacles to Germany reaching an understanding with other countries are the definition of an aggressor nation and how to designate an aggressor nation, which Germany opposes being decided by the League of Nations. In addition, political figures have also expressed the opinion that if Ambassador Ribbentrop can bring back a proposal from his government regarding the definition of an aggressor nation that is acceptable to all parties concerned when he returns to his post, then his country's opposition to the new Locarno Treaty and the Franco-Soviet mutual assistance pacts will also be eased accordingly. However, this approach is only a hope and should not be overly optimistic. (24th Havas Dispatch)

France's Attitude Towards Germany's Colonial Demands: A Genuine Solution to General European Problems as the Price of Exchanging Colonies

(London) The Times published a dispatch from its Paris correspondent today discussing France's attitude towards Germany's demands for colonies and non-intervention in the Spanish conflict. It briefly stated that if Germany is prepared to solve general European problems in a practical way as the price of exchanging colonies, then France should naturally agree to give colonies to Germany. Conversely, if Germany's demand for colonies is only to flaunt the power of the Nazi Party, then France has decided not to make any sacrifices. In short, although France is prepared to hold negotiations at any time to resolve Western European problems, it is not willing to use the colonial issue as a stepping stone for negotiations and thereby trigger discussions on other agreements. In France's view, Germany should first change its policies, abandon its threats and intimidation, and replace them with security guarantees. It should abandon its plans for large-scale rearmament and replace them with disarmament and arms control. Only then can France make some concessions to Germany on the colonial issue. However, such concessions by France must also be accompanied by sacrifices from other countries, because France is not the country that has benefited the most since the war. Even if Germany no longer has any demands on the countries of the world, its current interference in the Spanish conflict is more than enough to promote war. The nature of this matter is important and surpasses other events. German leader Hitler has repeatedly declared his aim is peace, so he should make every effort to avoid this interference. Therefore, French Foreign Minister Delbos is said to have informed the German government that if Germany intensifies its aid to the Spanish rebels and provides it with substantive assistance, then France will not be able to consistently adopt a non-intervention policy. In addition, The Times' Paris correspondent has also obtained reliable information to believe that French Foreign Minister Delbos has instructed the French Ambassador to the United Kingdom, Corbin, to suggest to the British government that the UK and France should jointly declare to Germany that the UK cannot tolerate Germany's actual invasion of Spain. The UK and France believe that this move by Germany is the beginning of disaster, and its intention is clearly to change the military strategic situation in the European Mediterranean, so that Germany can gain the upper hand in future wars. It is very clear that this kind of action will not prompt the UK and France to give some land to Germany, so that the country can use it as an outpost for engaging in war. (22nd Havas Dispatch)

Little Change in the Situation of the War in Spain; Rebel Aircraft Continue to Drop Bombs; Cannon Fire Can Be Heard Throughout the City

Madrid: There has been little change in the war situation in the vicinity of this city. The position of the government forces has only slightly improved in the town of Usera. The two armies exchanged fire today, and the cannon fire could be heard throughout the city. Three three-engine aircraft and six fighter planes of the Nationalist army bombed the positions of the government forces, but were chased away by government aircraft. The telephone company building in the capital, where journalists from various countries compile their reports, was again bombarded by Nationalist artillery today, but there was no significant damage. (23rd Havas Dispatch)

Madrid: Nationalist aircraft continued to bomb the Madrid telephone exchange today, attempting to cut off Spain's communication with the outside world. The exchange was hit by four bombs in ten minutes. One bomb penetrated the ceiling of the thirteenth floor, with a diameter of six feet. Another bomb destroyed the terrace of the twelfth floor. Several other bombs hit apartments in Gran Via, the Church of San Martin, Ampate Quay, and houses in Bilbao. (23rd National Dispatch)

Salamanca: According to the official Nationalist army bulletin issued last night, the town of Merida, 25 miles from the front line of Madrid, was bombed by government aircraft yesterday, killing 25 people and wounding 48. It also stated that the town of Merida is not a military stronghold. (24th Reuters Dispatch)

Negotiations for Exchange of Hostages Break Down

Saint-Jean-de-Luz: The hope of exchanging 4,000 detainees held as hostages by the warring parties in Spain before Christmas has been dashed due to the breakdown of negotiations. After many discussions, the representatives of the two sides have reached a complete stalemate. The main difficulty in the discussion is the age of military service. This afternoon, a British warship arrived here from Bilbao, carrying only a small number of refugees and no released hostages, which caused considerable disappointment to the welcomers on the dock. (23rd Reuters Dispatch)

American Socialists Prepare to Go to Spain to Help in the War

(New York) News today that a team of American Socialist Party members will soon go to Madrid to attack the Fascist forces in Spain. The team members include aviators, engineers, various technicians, artillery, and cavalry specialists, who will assist the International Brigades in carrying out operations in the vicinity of the capital of Spain. (23rd National Dispatch)

Portugal Expands Air Force; Purchases Large Number of Aircraft from Germany

Lisbon: The Portuguese government is actively expanding its air force and has ordered a large number of bombers and fighter planes from Germany. The first batch of ten three-engine bombers arrived here yesterday afternoon. Each plane can carry 40 to 50 people, 2,000 kilograms of bombs, is equipped with three machine guns, and can fly continuously for 1,200 kilometers. (24th Havas Dispatch)

France Builds Twelve Torpedo Boats

(Paris) The Navy Department is now building twelve new-style torpedo boats at the port of Dunkirk in the north. Each boat has a displacement of 600 tons. The first of these will soon be completed and a launching ceremony will be held in the port. The second will be completed by the end of January next year. (24th Havas Dispatch)

Indian National Congress Generates Fierce Movement Against Coronation Welcome Ceremony

Bhilpo: The Indian National Congress, which had just opened, generated a fierce movement against the coronation welcome ceremony, but the result is difficult to predict because conservative Congressmen are strongly opposed. He Jingwu Arrives in Jinan; Will Meet with Song After Visiting Han, Then Head to Ping

Jinan Correspondence: Mr. He Jingwu left Beijing on the 21st and took the Pingpu train north, arriving in Jinan at 10:00 a.m. on the 22nd. Chairman Han sent Zhang Cheng from the Provincial Committee to welcome him at the station. After Mr. He got off the train, he stayed at the Jinpu Railway Hotel to rest. Then, accompanied by Zhang Cheng, he toured Jinan's market streets and the road on the city wall. At 11:30 a.m., he went to the Provincial Government to meet with Chairman Han and attended a banquet hosted by Han. He had a lengthy conversation with Han in the office. Chairman Han expressed great concern for Chairman Chiang and said that he would support any good proposals and would do his best if needed. He would follow the Central Government in everything. Mr. He left the Provincial Government at 1:30 p.m. and took the Jinpu train 202 to Ping at 8:18 p.m. to meet with Chairman Song. He plans to stay in Ping for three or two days before returning to Beijing to report. Before Mr. He left Jinan, the reporter visited him and asked about the purpose of his visit and the results of his meeting with Chairman Han. I was granted an audience and recorded the following conversation:

He Jingwu's Talk

"The Xi'an Incident was completely unexpected. The entire country is extremely anxious and hopes for a swift resolution and the early rescue of Chairman Chiang. I have been traveling back and forth between Beiping, Luoyang, and Nanjing these past six or seven days, without any free time, which has made me feel unwell. I have not yet recovered. This trip north is to visit friends in a private capacity and to meet with Chairman Han of Shandong and Chairman Song of Beiping. I have known both Chairman Han and Chairman Song for a long time. Chairman Han has met me in Ping several times and invited me to visit Shandong, but I have been unable to accept due to work. Later, Shi Tang passed through Jinan, but he was also unable to get off the train due to being busy. I am very happy to have this opportunity to visit Chairman Han and reminisce about the old days. During the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army in 1928, I served as the Transportation Commander, leading the armored car team to Jinan. I only stayed for one day, and then the May 3rd Incident occurred and I was forced to leave Jinan. I lived on the train for six days and left with great pain. It has been ten years since I came to Jinan again. In recent years, under the leadership of Chairman Chiang, the country's political construction has been thriving, and the country's future is very promising. Unexpectedly, Zhang Xueliang suddenly launched a coup in Xi'an, kidnapping Chairman Chiang, which aroused unanimous opposition from the entire country. When I left Beijing, I had not heard the news of Chairman Song (Ziwen) returning to Beijing. I have read in the newspapers that Chairman Song has returned to Beijing. Madame Chiang Song Meiling is naturally even more worried about Chairman Chiang's safety. Even if someone tries to stop her, I am afraid she must go to Xi'an. When Jiang Dingwen left Xi'an and passed through Luoyang, I met with him and talked for a long time. Jiang did not know Zhang's true intentions. Zhang also knew that Chiang was in danger and that he himself would hardly escape. He told Chiang Dingwen to tell everyone to absolutely ensure Chairman Chiang's safety and believed that Chairman Chiang was in no danger. Zhang's actions against the will of the people will ultimately fail. The fact that the country has remained exceptionally stable in the midst of this crisis shows the progress of the nation and the people, which is truly gratifying. After arriving in Jinan this morning, I was greeted at the station by Chairman Han's representative, Chairman Zhang Bingqian. After getting off the train, I toured the streets of Jinan and felt that Shandong, under the leadership of Chairman Han, has made great progress in construction and the local area is extremely peaceful, which I deeply admire. At noon, I went to the Provincial Government to visit Chairman Han. After talking with the Chairman for a long time, we both felt that there were no specific measures to rescue Chairman Chiang. Chairman Han said that he would support any opinions and do his best wherever he was needed, and that he would follow the Central Government's policies in everything. I also felt that the news media in various places should contact the local newspapers to print additional copies and send them to Luoyang to be delivered by air to Xi'an by the Commander of the Air Force, Mao Bangchu, to let Zhang Hanqing understand public opinion and realize his mistake as soon as possible. I think this move will definitely be effective."

Yu Hanmou Sends Li Xuhuan to Beijing by Air to Request Instructions; Zou Lu Forcibly Travels to Beijing to Discuss National Affairs; Zhang Renmin Accompanies Deng Shizeng to Guilin

Guangzhou Correspondence: After the Shaanxi Incident, the authorities in Guangdong and Guangxi made efforts to maintain local security. In addition to issuing a telegram to express his attitude, Yu Hanmou, the Pacification Commissioner of Guangdong Province, also reported on the Shaanxi Incident at the joint military and political memorial week on the 21st. He solemnly declared that unified resistance to aggression is the unanimous demand of the whole country, and that those who violate the above requirements and obstruct the safety of the leader will be abandoned by the people of the whole country. Yu originally planned to go to Beijing to request instructions from the Central Government on the major plan for maintaining security, but because it was the winter defense period and defense was important, he could not spare the time. Therefore, he sent Li Xuhuan, Director of the Political Training Department of the Fourth Route Army, by air on the 20th, via Jiangxi Province, to Beijing, to represent him in reporting on the recent military and political situation in Guangdong Province and to request instructions on future policies.

Zou Lu, the President of Zhongshan University, had been living in seclusion to recuperate after returning from Europe following the renewal of the situation in Guangdong. He had not been involved in the affairs of Zhongshan University for a long time. His place of recuperation was first at Nengren Temple on Baiyun Mountain in the suburbs of Xi Zhou, then he moved to the Hot Springs area of Conghua County, and recently he has been hiding in an ancient temple on Mount Luofu. He has changed his place of recuperation three times and seemed to have not heard about the current situation for a long time. However, after the occurrence of the Shaanxi Incident, Zou's long-term illness had improved slightly. On the 21st, he attended the Zhongshan University Memorial Week, convened all the faculty and students to give instructions, and told them that the current situation was serious, and the students should implement their past proposals and jointly bear the responsibility of resisting aggression and saving the country. Zou also told reporters that after the Shaanxi Incident, the Central Government immediately telegraphed him to go to Beijing to discuss national affairs. Zhang Xueliang's rash action was extremely regrettable. He had to travel to Beijing with all his might to discuss effective methods with his comrades in the Central Government to assist Sui and rescue Chairman Chiang. On the 22nd, Zou, along with six or seven attendants, took the early morning ferry from Guangdong and Hong Kong to Hong Kong to wait for a boat to Shanghai and then to Beijing.

Regarding the attitude of Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi in Guangxi towards the Shaanxi Incident, two telegrams have already been sent. It is said that Li Pinxian was also planning to fly to Guangdong to exchange opinions some days ago, but it has not been possible due to weather conditions. It is said that Li will be able to fly to Guangzhou on the 22nd. Zhang Renmin, the staff officer of the Guangxi Army who led the Guangxi military and political inspection delegation some days ago, hurriedly passed through Guangdong the other day and went to Hong Kong, intending to lead the inspection delegation north. However, due to the situation, it was terminated. The Guangxi inspection delegation is now temporarily staying in Hong Kong awaiting orders. Zhang returned to Guangdong from Hong Kong again on the 20th, stayed in Guangdong for one day and night, and accompanied Deng Shizeng, the chief adviser of the Fourth Route Army, to Guilin by plane on the 21st to report to Li and Bai and to coordinate everything. (December 22nd)

The Pseudo Southeast Special Committee on the Border of Hunan, Hubei and Jiangxi has Disintegrated; More Than Eighty Pseudo County, District and Township-Level Organs Have Been Uncovered One After Another

Nanchang Correspondence: The counties of Wanzai, Yifeng, Pingjiang, Liuyang, Yangxin, Tonggu, Wuning, and Pingxiang in the combined area of Jiangxi, Hubei and Hunan provinces are surrounded by mountains and have complicated terrain. The remnant bandits under Xu Yigang, Fang Buzhou, and Yan Tuguo, based in places such as Huangjin Cave, constantly roamed the borders of northwestern Jiangxi, eastern Hunan, and southern Hubei. Under the command of Xiong Bin, the Commander of the Jiangxi Northwestern Anti-Banditry Campaign, the First and Second Security Regiments and the 708th Regiment of the 36th Brigade were divided into two columns to advance. They advanced from Yifeng towards the Hunan-Hubei border and recovered Huangjin Cave. In order to completely eliminate the remnant bandits, the department established political training sub-groups in the border areas of the bandit-suppression counties, and established model guerrilla groups under the sub-groups. These groups absorbed repentant elements to infiltrate the bandit forces for reconnaissance in order to uncover various secret organs of the bandits, which has been effective. Xiong Bin has reported to the Anti-Banditry Command of the Pingxiang Jiangxi-Hunan Border Region on the progress of bandit suppression. The progress is recorded as follows: "It has been found that three parts military and seven parts political is the only strategy for bandit suppression. Since its establishment in August this year, in addition to strictly supervising the troops to actively suppress the bandits, in terms of party and government, we have assisted the county magistrates of various counties to work hard. In order to increase efficiency, this headquarters has established political training groups in Wanzai, Pingxiang, Xiushui, Tonggu, Yifeng, Gaoan, Fengxin, Jingan, Wuning and other counties. Political training sub-groups were established in the border areas, all of which were directly under the command of the political training group of this headquarters. The main task is to eliminate remnant bandits, eliminate internal spies, improve mass organizations, awaken the anesthetized masses, convert to the Three People's Principles, thoroughly expose the bandit party's means of deceiving the masses, and crush the bandit party's internal and external organizations at all levels. Each sub-group is attached to a model guerrilla group (i.e. armed plainclothes team) for suppressing reactionaries, searching for scattered bandits, and covering the work of the sub-group. This system is actually the first of its kind since the launch of the suppression in this province, and it is also the most effective strategy for suppressing scattered bandits. Although the establishment of the sub-groups in the counties has been gradual, the statistics show that more than 80 pseudo county, district and township-level organs in various places have been uncovered, with 600 to 700 members of pseudo organizations, more than 100 captured, recruited, and killed red bandit cadres, and a large number of guns and various reactionary documents have been seized. The pseudo Southeast Special Committee, which occupied the border between Wanyi, Pingliu, and has been completely disintegrated."

Fujian Province: This Year's Budget Established, In Reality Still Deficit Spending

Fuzhou Correspondence: The budget proposal for the 25th year of the Republic of China in Fujian Province has now been compiled by the Provincial Government and submitted to the Executive Yuan for review and approval. Although the figures on paper show balanced income and expenditure, the reality is still deficit spending. This is because the income figures are based on the highest possible projections, which will certainly not be reached in the final accounting. The expenditure figures are based on the lowest possible projections, which will certainly be exceeded in the final accounting. Therefore, the provincial authorities are still making great efforts to rectify various taxes, such as conducting special investigations to clarify the reasons for the revenue shortfall. Starting from the 26th year, the system of contracted tax collection will be abolished to prevent tax collectors from enriching themselves. At the same time, all government agencies will be encouraged to economize on expenditures to reduce waste, only allowing for surpluses within the budgeted amount and not exceeding the original budget proposal. The main points of the local budget for the 25th year of this province are outlined below:

(A) Income Section

(1) Regular Revenue: Land tax 1,426,034 yuan, deed tax 600,000 yuan, business tax 2,815,993 yuan, house and shop tax 479,968 yuan, boat tax 207,712 yuan, local administrative revenue 503,197 yuan, local property income 112,000 yuan, subsidy income 2,156,556 yuan, other income 220,000 yuan, totaling 9,827,838 yuan. (2) Temporary Revenue: Collection fee 182,252 yuan, stamp tax 595 yuan, construction surtax 416,050 yuan, education surtax 411,354 yuan, security surtax 8,990.42 yuan, special business tax 2,237,386 yuan, central subsidy income 932,000 yuan, construction funds allocated by the National Economic Council (00,000 yuan, road construction subsidy income 180,000 yuan, other income 749,800 yuan, debt income 3,800,000 yuan, totaling 9,596,479 yuan.

(B) Expenditure Section

(1) Regular Expenditure: Party affairs expenses 151,490 yuan, administrative expenses 2,280,135 yuan, judicial expenses 800,160 yuan, public security expenses 4,163,000 yuan, financial expenses 1,017,084 yuan, education and cultural expenses 2,006,208 yuan, construction expenses 903,982 yuan, health expenses 261,920 yuan, assistance expenses 789,374 yuan, totaling 12,854,590 yuan. (2) Temporary Expenditure: Administrative expenses 129,360 yuan, construction expenses 986,930 yuan, assistance expenses 153,029 yuan, miscellaneous expenses 252,000 yuan, totaling 6,569,727 yuan.

As for the local income and expenditure of various counties and cities in the province, no budget proposals have been prepared in the past. In order to thoroughly reform the financial and administrative system of the province, the provincial government started the compilation and review of the local budgets of the counties and cities for the 15th year of the Republic of China in May and June of this year. The method was for each county and city government to compile a preliminary budget proposal based on the amount of local income and expenditure for this year and submit it to the province. The provincial government then handed it over to the Department of Finance to review it together with the relevant departments, bureaus, and offices. By September, all reviews were completed. However, at the beginning of this year, the financial and administrative systems and various taxes of the counties had undergone unprecedented changes. In order to accurately determine income and expenditure, the provincial government reissued the reviewed preliminary budget proposals to each county, ordering them to be provisionally implemented on a trial basis. If there were any comments, they were to be reported back within a limited time. Subsequently, the counties and cities successively reported back, and after the Department of Finance re-examined them, they were submitted to the provincial government committee for discussion in batches. Now, all have been approved. According to statistics, the total income and expenditure of 62 counties and one city is more than 8 million yuan. More than 120 kinds of miscellaneous taxes have been abolished, resulting in a reduction of more than 300,000 yuan. It can be said that the counties and cities of this province have only produced legally binding budget proposals this year. (23rd)

Baoding Fourth Prison: Political Prisoners Plot Escape, Guards Bribed to Allow Thugs to Enter Prison, Escapees Surrounded and Captured by Military and Police

Beiping Correspondence: Political prisoners in Baoding Fourth Prison have been actively plotting since the Shaanxi Incident, intending to take advantage of the opportunity to incite ordinary prisoners to jointly storm the prison. A guard named Wang Keren, having been bribed by people outside the prison, allowed four thugs to enter before the lockdown on the 22nd, mixing them in with the political prisoners. Each thug carried a firearm. At around 3:00 a.m. on the 23rd, they started an incident inside the prison, with all the prisoners rushing out. The guards' firearms were completely seized, and the office of the Second Section of the prison was surrounded. The on-duty chief guard, Zhao Xingwu, and the staff were driven into a corner of the room, and Zhao was forced to hand over the keys to each prison. Zhao refused and was severely injured. At that time, most of the prison gates were broken open by the prisoners, who rushed out and plundered more than 30 large rifles stored in the warehouse, carrying them out the gate, shouting slogans, and distributing leaflets. At this time, some staff of the prison and the chief of the Second Section, Zhou Kuiyuan, etc., escaped over the wall because the telephone lines were cut, and reported to the Hebei Provincial Security Office, Public Security Bureau, etc. Gao Shuxun, the deputy director of the Security Office, immediately dispatched a team to be on guard in the area of the east gate of the prison. At the same time, he quickly notified the 53rd Army to send two companies of soldiers and the Guards Battalion to send one company of soldiers to surround the prison. At around 4:00 a.m., the military, police, and constabulary had all arrived at the scene and made proper arrangements. When the thugs came out of the gate, they were intercepted by layers of military and police, and a fierce conflict immediately broke out. The thugs tried to rush out three times, but were all driven back. For a time, in order to prevent further incidents, the authorities ordered the traffic to be cut off, and the city gates were all tightly closed. The two sides confronted each other until around 6:00 a.m., when the authorities increased the number of reinforcements by dispatching two battalions of infantry from the 109th Brigade of the 37th Division and ordered them to climb the houses around the prison and press inward. At this point, the thugs began to surrender their weapons, and the escapees were captured one by one. By 7:30 a.m., the entire incident was resolved. By 9:00 a.m., the entire city had returned to normal.

After receiving the news of the prison storming in Baoding, Deng Zhexi, the president of the Hebei Provincial High Court, immediately went to Song's residence in Wuyi Ku Hutong to meet with Song and report the incident. Mr. Song was extremely furious and ordered that the lawless elements be dealt with by military law. At the same time, the prison warden, Ma Shixiong, and the security personnel were also severely punished for dereliction of duty. After Deng resigned, he convened a meeting at the High Court with Wu Shiyuan, warden of the First Prison, Tian Wenlie, warden of the Second Prison, and Wu Bingcheng, director of the Beiping Detention Center, to discuss the prevention measures for the prisons in Beiping. A decision was made after much discussion. After the meeting, Tianjin Third Prison and other prisons were also ordered to pay attention to prevention to avoid similar incidents from happening. In order to investigate the truth of the Baoding incident, Deng sent a Mr. Zhou to Baoding on the 23rd. Deng himself is also planning to go there in the next few days. (23rd)

Kunshan: Tea Shop Tragically Robbed by Bandits

Recently, robbery cases in various villages have been reported frequently. The Fuxin Tea and Food Shop in Binxi Township, Second District, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits at around 1:00 a.m. on the 22nd. The shop owner, Chen Baisheng, the maid, Yang, and the apprentices were tied up and beaten severely. The bandits then wantonly searched and looted the shop, resulting in a loss of more than 200 yuan in cash and other items. The case was reported to the county for investigation and pursuit, but the bandits had already fled far away.

Refugees Disturbing Villages and Towns

On the morning of the 23rd, more than 200 refugees arrived in the Huangjing area, which is the border area of Kunshan, Changshu, and Wujiang counties, disturbing the villages and towns in the area and occupying the local temple. The Fourth Branch Bureau of Bacheng in this county immediately reported the incident and, together with the County Bureau, the water patrol team, and the security team, rushed to the area to intercept and drive them out of the area.

Changshu: Xijing Traitor Captured in Zhitang

After the garrison stationed here arrested two traitors the other day and executed them, yesterday (the 23rd), the Zhitang Public Security Bureau arrested four more traitors at the train station. The traitors were disguised as chicken vendors and carried more than 20 chickens, male and female. They boarded a car at the Zhitang Bus Station. Because their actions were suspicious, they were identified by the police at the station. After questioning, they did not understand any of the jargon used by chicken vendors. They were immediately taken to the local Second Branch Bureau for detailed interrogation. They confessed their names as Gu Yulong (from Rugao), Li Xiuzhen, Liu Guangfa, and Wang Qiyou (all from Anhui). They directly admitted that they were being used by a certain party to come to Changshu to carry out reconnaissance work and investigate troop movements. Each person could get 1.4 yuan per day. This time, they came to Changshu for the second time, etc. After obtaining the confession, the branch bureau immediately sent them to the Public Security Bureau. The Supervisory Office, considering that the case was a serious crime involving traitors, secretly interrogated them again that night. It is reported that, except for Gu Yulong's cunning confession, the other three criminals have confessed without reservation. They will now be transferred to military law for trial.

Wuxi: Summoning Tu Zheng for Instruction

Because the major households in this county owed more than one million yuan in land tax, Su Caiying sent Dong Qicheng, a tax collection commissioner, to Wuxi to urge payment. After Dong arrived in Wuxi, he consulted with the Long County Chief several times on how to recover the arrears. The matter was completed yesterday and he returned to the province. Currently, the county government has decided to summon all the Tu Zheng and tax collectors of the county on the 29th of this month to the county for instruction, instructing them to make efforts to collect taxes and ensure that 600,000 yuan must be collected in the shortest possible time. If there is any delay, they will be dealt with according to law. As for the years for which arrears are being collected, the focus is on the taxes owed from the 20th to the 24th years of the Republic of China.

Jiangyin: Hunger Strike by Prisoners

The prisoners in the county prison and detention center are protesting over the issue of food rations. According to regulations, each prisoner is supposed to receive one jiao of silver per day, with a meal weighing 24 taels. Recently, the amount of food has been reduced. Yesterday (the 23rd) at 3:00 p.m., the prisoners rioted and refused to eat, causing great chaos. The warden, Tang Qimu, went to stop them, but they refused to listen to his advice. Tang A'bao, a prisoner awaiting trial for opium offenses, and Zhang Jinbao, an administrative detainee, were the most激烈。 They were taken out separately. At the same time, the county government was telephoned, and Tang Jien, the leader of the Second Platoon of the Security Team, led the team to suppress the riot and persuade them to eat as usual. The situation did not calm down until around 5:00 p.m.

Changzhou: Building a Ring Road

Hou Houzong, the county chief of Wujin County, said that the ring road in the county, except for the section near Qingliang Temple, which was built by public labor service in the 24th year of the Republic of China, the section from De'an Bridge eastward to Wuqing Road, and the section where the existing roadbed extends and connects to Wuyi Road, have not yet been completed. Yesterday, he specially ordered Zhao Changfeng, the district chief of the First District, to list this as a labor service project for the 25th year of the Republic of China in the district, and issued blueprints, etc., ordering him to immediately instruct the relevant township chiefs to supervise the strong men to start work on schedule and report the tools so that personnel can be dispatched at any time to guide the project.

Zhenjiang: Brothel Bathhouse Cracked Down

Li Yurong, the Baozhang of Menghu Township, No. 10 Xinximen Riverside in this port, runs a paper mill as his business. Recently, due to the arrival of the severe winter, business has been slow. Suddenly, he had a whim to build a small room in the store and secretly set up a women's bathhouse, enticing ignorant women to go to bathe. Each bath only cost five jiao of silver. The average woman was greedy for its cheap price, so they introduced each other and flocked to it. Little did they know that the bathhouse was not only poorly equipped and unsanitary, but also mixed men and women, which was a matter of morality. The incident was discovered by the Public Security Third Branch Bureau. Yesterday afternoon at 6:00 p.m., the Branch Bureau Chief Ji Zonghan led Patrol Officer Weng Zuyi and more than ten policemen to arrest them. At that time, the Kunqu opera actors Zuo Yunxia and Zuo Cai were bathing in the room, and a woman named Zhang was undressing outside the room, waiting to bathe. Seeing a large number of men in black entering, they were shocked and discolored. The Branch Bureau Chief Ji ordered those who had entered the bath to quickly put on their clothes and took them to the branch bureau for interrogation. It is heard that they will be transferred to the General Bureau for punishment.

Wanfu Bridge Completed

Wanfu Bridge in Jiangdu County, this province, has been destroyed by military service for a long time. The Jiangsu Construction Department believes that the bridge is a necessary thoroughfare for the Yangqing, Yangjing, and Yangpu roads. In August of this year, the Construction Department allocated funds and specially dispatched engineers to supervise the construction. Now, it has been fully completed. The road surface paving on the roads connected to the bridge has been completed one after another, and all can be opened to traffic.

Yangzhou: Woman Heartbroken and Dying

Guan Xueren, a tea servant at the Zhongnan Bank in Shanghai, from No. 7, Jia 6, Bao 10, Maqiao Township, Fourth District, Jiangdu, only has his wife Jiang, age 24. On the night of the 22nd, Li Yuanhai, a resident of the same village, suddenly broke open the gate and entered, hacking at Jiang's head and arms with a sharp axe and cutting off her right ear. At that time, the sound of screams spread to the neighbors, who rushed to check and rescue her. Jiang was already lying in a pool of blood, and Li was still holding the axe beside her. Jiang's father, Songlin, was notified and reported to the Winter Defense Office. The patrol team leader, Zhan Shucun, led the team to rush to the scene and arrested the murderer and the carpenter Chen Xiaoqi, who lent Li the axe, and sent them to Xianzhen. Currently, Jiang is dying after being injured. It is said that Li and Jiang had previously been in love, but Jiang followed her husband to Shanghai. Li once followed her, and Jiang told him to return to his hometown and talk about it again. This summer, Jiang returned, and always gave Li the cold shoulder. The seeds of disaster may have been planted here.

Nantong: Murderer Arrested in Tong

Zhang Wenwei, from Yuyao, was doing business in Shanghai. His son was defrauded of a huge sum of money by Shen Lishun and killed. Shen, the murderer, was arrested in Tong, and the corpse was exhumed and identified in a desolate grave. On the 23rd, the Nantong District Court concluded the trial of Shen Lishun and sentenced him to life imprisonment.

Jiaxing: Schools Stop Giving Winter Vacation

The county government stated that this year's winter vacation, according to the primary school layer regulations, will be given from January 18th to January 31st. However, during this year's winter vacation, it is appropriate for the second phase of mass training. Teachers and staff of primary schools at all levels mostly serve as political training instructors, bearing heavy responsibilities and unable to ask for leave. On the 24th, all primary schools in the county were ordered to stop giving winter vacation. All teachers and staff should stay in school and not listen to their own wishes. In addition to undertaking mass training political program, they must also conduct a thorough investigation of school-age children in the education area, so that the enrollment system can be promoted in the next semester.

Handling Rent Collection According to Previous Cases

In order to ensure the main source of land tax revenue for the first period of this year, the county government is using the Baojia system to strictly urge households to pay, in order to achieve results. It is also said that grain comes from rent, and the poor harvest of rent rice will damage the income from grain tax. Now, in order to take into account the collection of rent rice by industry households, it has been decided to follow previous cases and establish a rent collection office in the county from the winter solstice, where industry households can apply for the recovery of unpaid rent rice from tenants in accordance with the regulations.

Hangzhou: Strict Handling of County Chief in Lost City Case

The county town of Changhua was recently captured by bandits, and the county government, the Party headquarters, and many houses were burned down, resulting in huge local losses. The provincial government, considering that the county chief, Yu Mingchang, had left his post without permission and stayed in the provincial capital, detained him and transferred him to the Zhejiang High Court for trial in accordance with the law. The criminal division of the court once held a trial. Yu's testimony was evasive, and he was sent to the detention center and prosecuted by the court for dereliction of duty and strictly handled.

Conscripting Strong Men to Fill the Seawall

For the Zhejiang Provincial National Labor Service Project to Fill the Seawall, more than 2,000 strong men have been conscripted near the Cao'e River in the Shaoxiao section and are starting work. Xiaoshan County is rushing to conscript 3,000 strong men and is scheduled to start work on the 25th. It is also heard that the grout engineering of the Jia Yan Stone Seawall will begin within days once the machinery is delivered.

Shaoxing: Implementing Winter Defense Patrols

Recently, the county government has stated that the situation is unstable, and it is inevitable that villains will take the opportunity to stir up trouble. In order to maintain local security, winter defense is being implemented. In addition to increasing the number of police patrols on night shifts, security teams are also dispatched to guard the main roads. After 12:00 midnight, pedestrians must have a winter defense pass to be allowed to pass. In the areas near the city, multi-area joint defense patrols are being implemented.

Local News

Representatives from All Circles Held a Grand Meeting Yesterday to Support the Central Government in Punishing the Rebels; Over Two Thousand Five Hundred Representatives from Various Groups Attended; All Vowed Allegiance to the Party and the Nation and Supported Chairman Chiang

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, in order to uphold the central government in punishing the rebels Zhang Xueliang, who betrayed the Party and the nation, hijacked the supreme commander, detained generals who were suppressing the Communists and resisting the enemy, and obstructed the defense against humiliation and national salvation, specially convened a grand meeting of representatives from all circles at the City Chamber of Commerce Auditorium at 2:00 PM yesterday to support the central government in punishing the rebels. Important proposals were also passed. The details are recorded below:

Representatives Present

Including Wu Xianxian, Tao Baichuan, and Pan Gongzhan from the Municipal Party Headquarters; Wu Tiecheng from the Municipal Government (represented by Zhou Yongneng); Yang Hu from the Garrison Headquarters; Zhou Xuexiang and Zhu Xuefan from the Lu Jingshi General Labor Union; Tong Xingbai from the Boy Scouts Council; Huang Zaoxiong from the Education Association; Zhang Shouyong from the New Life Movement Promotion Association; Du Yuesheng and Wang Kui Sheng from the Local Association; Wang Xiaolai and Jin Runyang from the City Chamber of Commerce; Yu Zhenhui from the City Morning Association; Cai Jinjun and Liang Fuchu from the Public Security Bureau; as well as representatives from various agencies, groups, schools, and Party departments at all levels, including Liu Heqin, Huang Xianggu, Zhang Yunzeng, and Yu Yaoqiu, totaling more than two thousand five hundred people, with Wu Tiecheng (represented by Zhou Yongneng), Pan Gongzhan, Cai Jinjun, Tong Xingbai, Lu Jingshi, Zhang Shouyong, Du Yuesheng (represented by Wang Kui Sheng), Zhu Xuefan, Huang Zaoxiong, Yu Zhenhui, and Pan Gongbi as the twelve members of the presidium.

Meeting Order

(1) Opening of the meeting; (2) Playing of the national anthem; (3) Paying respects to the Party, the nation, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen; (4) Reading the Last Will and Testament of Sun Yat-sen; (5) Observing three minutes of silence for the martyrs who died in the Xi'an Incident; (6) Chairman's report; (7) Speeches; (8) Discussion of proposals; (9) Shouting slogans; (10) Playing music; (11) Adjournment of the meeting.

After the rituals were completed, Chairman Pan Gongzhan delivered a speech, stating that the representatives from all walks of life in Shanghai are holding this meeting to support the central government in punishing the rebels. All representatives have come to participate, and they must have two kinds of feelings: (1) Infinite pain and indignation at Zhang Xueliang's rebellion in Xi'an. At a time when peace and unification have been achieved internally and the war of resistance against the enemy is beginning externally, Zhang Xueliang, driven by madness, hijacked our national leader, causing great damage to all the great undertakings of national construction and rejuvenation, both internally and externally. This is truly the public enemy of our entire nation and a matter of great pain and indignation. (2) Showing great strength. However, Zhang was completely unrepentant. People across the country, regardless of their position, expressed great indignation and unanimously applied to the central government to punish him. After this incident, we can fully demonstrate the organized and united spirit of our country. Everyone should wholeheartedly support the central government, implement national policies, support the hardworking and meritorious Chairman Chiang, punish the rebel Zhang Xueliang, and strive for the revolution. We will surely achieve the final victory, and the great cause of saving the country and rejuvenation will surely be completed.

Today is the Anniversary of the Yunnan Uprising; All Circles Hold a Commemorative Meeting; The Yunnan Fellow Association Holds a Celebration Meeting; Banks and Money Shops are Closed for One Day

Today is the 21st anniversary of the Yunnan Uprising. The Municipal Party Department of this city has specially scheduled a commemorative meeting at 10:00 AM today in the auditorium of the department. The Yunnan Fellow Association in Shanghai will also hold a celebration meeting at the YMCA in the Baixianqiao at 3:00 PM today. All organs, groups, and schools in the city will hang flags to celebrate, and the Bankers Association, the Money Industry Association, and all banks and money shops will be closed.

The Garrison Headquarters Issued a Public Notice Yesterday Maintaining Public Order; Illegal Parades, Demonstrations, Strikes, and Class Strikes Will Be Dealt with According to Military Law Once Discovered

The Songhu Garrison Headquarters issued a public notice yesterday to strictly maintain local order. The notice from Nantong stated: After the Xi'an Incident occurred, martial law has been ordered to be declared in this city, and it has been announced on record. However, Songhu is located in a strategic area where Chinese and foreigners live together, and it is still feared that bad elements will move around and try to achieve their goals. Therefore, we are sincerely informing you again that if anyone spreads rumors, disturbs public order, destroys finance, infringes on foreigners, or illegally assembles, forms societies, parades, demonstrates, strikes, or boycotts classes in this city, they will be dealt with according to military law once discovered. In addition to ordering all military police to conduct strict investigations at all times, it is imperative to announce it to the public for their information, and all sectors of society must abide by it and not violate it. This is a close announcement, December 24th, 25th year of the Republic of China, Commander Yang Hu.

Mr. Shi Fang Geng and Ms. Zhu Yunqing Held a Grand Ceremony Yesterday

Mr. Shi Yonggeng, former chief editor of this newspaper, was introduced by Mr. Du Yuesheng and Mr. Wang Xiaolai two years ago and became engaged to Ms. Zhu Yunqing, the sister of Mr. Zhu Douwen and Mr. Zhu Rushan. Yesterday, the wedding ceremony was held at the Pudong Fellow Association. Mayor Wu was invited to witness the wedding. Both parties agreed to simplify and economize due to the seriousness of the national crisis, and they will not send invitations to relatives and friends separately.

Italian Ambassador to China, Luo Yagu Nuo, visited Beijing to inquire about the Xi'an Incident and express his condolences to Chairman Chiang. After staying in Beijing for two days, he visited Dean Kong on the afternoon of the day before yesterday and left Beijing on the 11:00 PM night express train and returned to Shanghai.
