Lixin Accounting Tutorial School Adds Day School

The Lixin Accounting Tutorial School on Jiangxi Road originally had night school, morning school, Sunday school, and correspondence school, etc. Since its establishment, it has been through nine years, and the number of students has reached more than 6,000. However, the night school and morning school are specially designed for the after-work tutoring of staff from all walks of life in Shanghai. For students who have not yet been employed, or who have come to the school from other places in China and abroad specifically to study, they feel that the study period is too long and uneconomical. At the same time, in recent years, students who are studying or have graduated from junior high school, high school, and university have been requesting the addition of a day school in increasing numbers. The school, in view of the urgent social need, decided to open a day school from February 26th. In addition to teaching the necessary knowledge and skills of accounting, it also offers subjects related to accounting, while also emphasizing extracurricular practice, striving to enable students to complete the main courses of the business school and accounting department of the university in a short period of two or three semesters. It is reported that the school's day school is divided into three levels: junior, middle, and senior high school, each level is one semester, and applicants must have a secondary school education and pass the entrance examination. The charter and application forms will be sent immediately upon request.

Special Issue Commemorating the Fourth Anniversary of New Cosmos Vocational School, Middle School, Elementary School, and Second Elementary School

Preface

— Zhang Xinbo

Our school was established four years ago in the blink of an eye. During these four years, thanks to the guidance and supervision of the educational authorities, the support and encouragement of people from all walks of life, and the hard work and cooperation of the school board, faculty, and students, we have achieved today's results. Such as expanding school buildings, enriching equipment, adding departments, increasing classes, raising the level of students, paying attention to student training, conducting research work, and promoting supplementary education, although it has been a difficult creation and a painstaking management, all the progress has been in accordance with the predetermined plan, resolutely implemented, and has been filed with the Shanghai Education Bureau and the Ministry of Education, which is what Xinbo and others are comforted by.

However, the education cause is a century-long plan. The future of New Cosmos is just beginning. In the future, we should work harder to raise funds to build new school buildings, continue to enrich equipment, and strive for progress as needed by the times, in order to make greater contributions to the future of education in our country and the revival of the nation. Zhuangzi said: "The beginning is simple, but the end will be great." It is even more necessary for the educational authorities to continue their guidance and supervision, for people from all walks of life to enthusiastically support and encourage, and for the school board, faculty, and students to work harder and cooperate.

As the fourth anniversary approaches, we are compiling and printing a special issue, briefly describing the past situation, the current state, and the future plans of our school, in order to seek correction from the virtuous and wise of the world, and also to commemorate the past and encourage the future.

New Cosmos in the Past Four Years

— (Zhang Zhonghuan)

"New Cosmos" has been around for four years since it was born. Taking advantage of the fourth anniversary, I will make a brief description of the progress in the past four years, which is also to review the implementation of the past and encourage the efforts of the future.

Chairman of the Board Jiang Wenyu

(1) The Purpose of Founding the School

(1) School education should strive for universality; however, there are few schools in our country, and less than 20% of children attend school. Our school is to run a school with private funds to supplement the inadequacy of national education. And to seek the quantitative development of education.

(2) There are very few schools in our country that meet the standards and are well-managed, and it is very appropriate to run a private school. At present, due to the limitations of manpower and financial resources, our school is inevitably simple and crude, and is still far from the ideal standard, but we always hope to make progress step by step and become an ideal and perfect private school, and to seek the qualitative improvement of education.

Founder and Principal Zhang Bo

(3) Educational ideals and teaching methods must rely on practical experience to be effective. However, public schools are often affected by the situation and restricted by laws and regulations, and cannot have the slightest freedom; our school can make appropriate adjustments under the national education policy and regulations, in order to better adapt to the actual situation. And test the actual problems of education.

(4) Middle school graduates often lack considerable knowledge and skills, and cannot adapt to the needs of society, and their character and temperament flow into frivolousness and laziness; if the school has one more graduate, society will add one unemployed person, and the family will have one less useful child? It will be seen that the more popular education is, the greater the harm to public and private life. If we want to realize the claim of education to save the country, we must correct this malpractice, promote vocational education, and pay attention to production training. This is why our school has the motivation to found a vocational school.

Founder and Principal Zhang Zhonghuan

(2) Quantitative Development

(1) Increase in Departments This school only established the lower grades of elementary school in the second semester of the twenty-first year; in the twenty-second year, it added the middle and upper grades and kindergarten, and added a junior commercial vocational school; in the twenty-third year, the vocational school added a junior applied chemistry department, senior business department, and electrical engineering department, and the elementary school added a second elementary school, which is a junior single-grade elementary school. In the twenty-fourth year, the senior electrical engineering department was changed to a senior applied chemistry department, and the second elementary school was added with senior grades and kindergarten; this semester, a junior middle school was added.

(2) Addition of Classes This school only established one class in the lower grades in the second semester of the twenty-first year, experimenting with individual teaching methods; in the first semester of the twenty-second year, the elementary school increased to four classes, and the vocational school established one class in the first grade of the junior commercial department, a total of five classes; in the second semester, the elementary school and vocational school each increased one class, a total of seven classes; in the twenty-third year, the elementary school added another class, totaling six classes, and the vocational school also increased to six classes, and a first elementary school was established with one class in the junior single grade, totaling thirteen classes; in the first semester of the twenty-fourth year, the vocational school increased to nine classes, and the second elementary school increased to six classes, totaling seven classes; a total of twenty-two classes; in the second semester, the second elementary school added four classes, totaling twenty-six classes; this semester, the vocational school increased to eleven classes, and a first-year junior middle school class was added, totaling twenty-nine classes.

(3) Increase in Students The school only had more than 20 students in the elementary school in the second semester of the twenty-first year; in the first semester of the twenty-second year, the vocational school was added, and the number of students reached 100; in the second semester, it increased to more than 150; in the twenty-third year, there were a total of 250 students in the middle and elementary schools; in the first semester of the twenty-fourth year, it increased to more than 700; in the second semester, it increased to more than 800; this semester, the total number of students in all departments will be close to 1,000.

(4) Increase in Teachers and Staff There were only two teachers and staff in the second semester of the twenty-first year; in the first semester of the twenty-second year, there were sixteen; in the second semester, there were twenty-four; in the twenty-third year, there were twenty-nine teachers and staff in the vocational school and ten teachers and staff in the elementary school, totaling thirty-nine; in the first semester of the twenty-fourth year, there were thirty-eight teachers and staff in the vocational school and seventeen teachers and staff in the elementary school, totaling fifty-five; in the second semester, the elementary school increased by five teachers and staff, totaling sixty; this semester, the vocational school increased to forty-eight teachers and staff, and the elementary school increased to twenty-one teachers and staff, totaling sixty-nine.

(3) Material Enrichment

(1) Expansion of School Buildings The school building in the second semester of the twenty-first year was on Lafayette Road, Lafayette Lane, which was very small. From the twenty-second year, it moved to the intersection of Pike Road and Special Road, and added two dormitories nearby. In the twenty-third year, the original site on Pike Road was used exclusively for elementary school, and the vocational school was moved to the intersection of Jianwei Road and Kangti Road, and a dormitory was rented nearby, and the first elementary school was added. In the twenty-fourth year, because the place was small and insufficient to accommodate, and could not be developed, the vocational school and the second elementary school were moved to the current address at No. 270 Chongqing Road. In the first semester, a Western-style house at No. 112 Weihaiwei Road was rented as a lower-grade classroom for the elementary school. This semester, a new auditorium was built, which can accommodate 700 to 800 people.

(2) Increase in School Equipment The school equipment has been added year by year to meet actual needs; since the increase in the number of people from 1931, more has been added. In terms of teaching equipment, such as new-style iron-legged desks and chairs, standard blackboards, pianos, organs, Chinese and English typewriters, computers, arithmetic teaching aids, history and geography maps, natural science maps, and military toys for children, everything has been enriched.

Part of the Faculty and Students of Our School (Half of it was cut off due to the relationship of the manufacturing relationship)

(3) Addition of Books In addition to the donation of more than 2,000 books by the founder, the school also designates special funds every semester to add books. Recently, the elementary school has also ordered the Elementary School Student Library, the Children's Library, the Elementary School Student Supplementary Readers, the Little Friend's Library, and the Elementary School Textbooks and Small World for each subject. The vocational school has reordered the Twenty-Five Histories, the Congshu Jicheng, the Wanyou Wenku, the First and Second Series, the Ministry of Publications, the Chemical Industry Series, the Junior High School Student Library, the Basic Knowledge Series, and many other great works.

(4) Increase in Instruments The school already has a rough model for physics instruments, chemical instruments and reagents, and museum specimens. Due to the addition of senior grades and the addition of applied chemistry departments, the instruments and reagents have been added to a greater extent. In the future, it is planned to increase purchases year by year to gradually achieve perfection.

(5) Expansion of Practice Since the school added the business department, it has paid attention to commercial practice, and has successively added practice shops, practice banks, commodity showrooms, Chinese and English typing rooms, and statistical practice rooms for students to study, practice, and practice on weekdays; in recent years, it has gradually tried to enrich them. The shops and banks are roughly scaled, and the commodity showroom is divided into two parts, domestic goods and foreign goods, for research and identification. There are currently six Chinese typewriters and twenty-four English typewriters. In the future, it is planned to add several more machines each semester, so that students can have more opportunities to practice; it is planned to go to several large companies and banks to allow students to have the opportunity to practice on the spot before graduation (in recent years, they have practiced in the Commercial Press and Zhonghua Book Company, etc., and the results are very good, and have been praised). As for the applied chemistry department, in the autumn of the twenty-third year, it jointly established a factory with the Oriental Instrument Company at Gaochang Temple Xinzhaozhou Road in Nanshi, which is divided into woodworking, casting, forging, fitter, and metalworking workshops for students to practice. Last year, the school building was moved, which was inconvenient for commuting. In addition to doing a long-term practice in the factory before graduation, another workshop was opened in the school, which is divided into two parts: metal and woodworking and applied chemistry workshops. All the workshop equipment is also gradually added to make it complete.

(4) Content Improvement

(1) Improving the Level of Students In recent years, schools at all levels often focus on form and activities, resulting in a general downward trend in the level of students. Therefore, the school pays great attention to the compilation of the curriculum, the distribution of teaching materials, and the selection of textbooks; it also pre-orders outlines of the curriculum for each subject, improves the teaching methods for each subject, encourages teachers to continue their studies; and pays serious attention to the examination of grades, extracurricular research, teaching equipment, and guidance on study and career; therefore, the level of students is gradually improving.

(2) Training Professional Knowledge and Skills The vocational school pays special attention to the training of professional knowledge and skills. Such as emphasizing practice and exercises, conducting professional lectures, and conducting special research, etc., to ensure that students have specialized knowledge and skills after graduation, not enough to make a living for individuals, but enough to revive the country and the people.

(3) Determining Training Objectives The school deeply feels that the scope of education is not only to impart knowledge, so it attaches great importance to student training on weekdays. Looking at the general public in our country, they are ignorant and ignorant, and most of them have four common problems: "poverty", "weakness", "selfishness", and "scattered"; therefore, the school's training objectives are to cultivate production knowledge and skills, to forge a sound physique, to cultivate a noble personality, and to pay attention to discipline training, in order to remedy the withering of the people's livelihood, the weakness of the physique, the lack of public morality, and the scattered spirit; and in the implementation of this, based on the psychology of young people and children, we pay attention to personality influence and adopt positive guidance to train sound citizens.

(4) Cultivating Patriotic Spirit In recent times, the people's morale has been low and life has been decadent. Most people only know how to be selfish and self-interested, and follow the old ways. They lack the ability to be confident and self-aware, and they have no spirit of sacrifice and struggle, which has led to the weakening of national power and the urgency of foreign insults. The nation-state is in danger. Therefore, the school trains children and young people. Whether in teaching or guidance, we focus on cultivating students' national consciousness and patriotic spirit, so that they become loyal, courageous, striving, sacrificing, and public-spirited citizens, so that they can save the country and revive the nation.

Gate

(5) Paying Attention to Teaching Research The school was founded in order to engage in educational research and experimentation; however, in the past four years, we are ashamed that there are no concrete and satisfactory results. Recently, we are conducting investigations, visits, discussions, and experiments on the curriculum, teaching, equipment, and training; and we are starting to compile the New Cosmos Vocational Series, the New Cosmos Children's Series, and the National Hero Stories Series.

(5) Future Plans

(1) Raising Funds to Build New School Buildings The school site of the middle and elementary school departments is less than 1 mu, and there are only a few hundred school buildings. There are more than 900 students, and we feel that there is no room to accommodate them. Therefore, to make progress, we must raise funds to build new school buildings. In the future, it is planned to use the original vocational school and the second elementary school site exclusively for junior high school and the second elementary school, and then purchase 50 mu of land in the suburbs of Shanghai to build a classroom, two dormitories, an auditorium, and a factory, which is expected to cost 200,000 yuan and can accommodate 1,500 students, so as to become a more perfect vocational school. Before the purchase of land and construction are completed, we must still expand the school buildings to facilitate development.

One of the School Views

(2) Enriching Necessary Equipment The school has been adding equipment as much as possible every semester; in recent years, due to the increase in students, all desks, chairs, cabinets, books, instruments, and business practice equipment, applied agricultural science practice workshops, etc., have been purchased in large quantities, but this is still not enough to be considered rich; in the future, we must still allocate large sums of money every year and request subsidies from the Ministry of Education, specifically for the purchase of books, instruments, and commercial and applied chemistry practice equipment, etc., in order to exceed the standards set by the Ministry within three years and reach a perfect state.

(3) Adding Departments and Classes The school's vocational middle school currently has eleven classes. In the future, it is planned to add a civil engineering department, aiming to reach eighteen classes, so that the applied chemistry department, business department, and civil engineering department will all complete six grades each for senior and junior high school; each grade of junior high school will reach three grades, totaling nine grades; the New Cosmos Elementary School plans to gradually increase to ten grades, that is, eight grades for the first-grade dual-grade elementary school and two grades for senior high school; the second elementary school plans to increase to two grades in kindergarten and each grade of elementary school will reach three grades, totaling twenty grades; the total number of students will be 2,000.

(4) Promoting Supplementary Education Education is one of the social undertakings. The facilities of the school should be integrated with the society. If we run the school behind closed doors, it is definitely not the essence of education. Therefore, the school has always attached great importance to promoting supplementary education, and has held vocational supplementary schools in recent years, such as the Mandarin Specialization Department, the English Specialization Department, the Japanese Specialization Department, the Arithmetic Specialization Department, the Women's Supplementary Department, the Shop Assistant's Supplementary Department, the Chinese and English Typing Department, and the Chinese Shorthand Department, etc., and the tuition fees charged are very low. However, due to focusing on the progress of vocational middle school and elementary school, the supplementary school has not been able to make much progress. In the future, we must pay more attention to it in order to promote it and strive for popularization.

However, after four years of hard work and struggle, and painstaking management, New Cosmos has grown from a low-level single-grade elementary school to now having a kindergarten, a first elementary school, a second elementary school, a junior high school, and a junior and senior vocational school; from one class to now having twenty-nine classes; from more than twenty students to now having more than nine hundred students; from two teachers to now having more than sixty teachers; the speed of progress is truly amazing! However, the education cause is a century-long plan. The future development is great. In order to make a slight contribution to the nation and the country, we rely more on the enthusiastic support of people from all walks of life and the school board, and the joint efforts of teachers, staff, and students.

Business News

Yarn Flower: Triple Yarn Soars to the Limit, Local Yarn Falls and Returns

Yesterday, the yarn market initially saw sellers enthusiastically delivering goods, and the Japanese month was the last scene. 3,500 bales of yarn were unloaded into the warehouse the day before yesterday. According to people in the market, 3,700 bales were unloaded yesterday, totaling as many as 7,000 bales. The market was suppressed by this and mixed. Then, the China Cotton Company accepted all of them. In the afternoon, Osaka spot yarn also rose by 6.7 yuan to 11.15 yuan, and people's hearts were raised again, and market prices rebounded again. The momentum of this month is quite peaceful. The closing price was 263 yuan, up 16.9 yuan from the previous month.

Yarn Prices Influenced by Japanese Yarn

The pre-market opening of the standard yarn continued the rising trend from the closing of the previous day, and this month is the last day of operation, and it is said that there are as many as 4,000 to 5,000 bales to be delivered. However, all parties are prepared to scan and accept, so the market situation this month is firm and rising by 1.3 yuan. However, the forward period is looser and falls, but the large households have not given up on absorbing the amount, so the forward period's decline is still flat. The spot yarn situation is still good. The result of the standard yarn is that this month is up 8 cents from the closing price of the previous day, and the rest is down 9 cents to 2.4 yuan. In the afternoon, due to sufficient deliveries this month, the market was very weak, and the selling pressure was also strong, and it fell across the board. When bidding to the March period, the Osaka Telegraph futures were suspended. Spot yarn rose by 6.7 yuan, and line rose by 11 to 15 yuan. The market was turbulent. Many people said that the Toyo issued a public price of tens of thousands of dollars and were optimistic about the future of triple yarn. Each month rose by 89 cents to 1 yuan, until the three closing, this month stabilized, the forward period was slightly weak, and the result was that each month rose by 4.6.9 cents from the morning closing price, and this month fell by 8 cents. It was found that Yuda sold 2,150 bales, Dafeng 1,590 bales, Zhenda 500 bales, Hexing 1,500 bales, Wang Taixing 1,150 bales, Changfeng 5,050 bales, Dachang 2,900 bales, Fengtai 600 bales, and Taichang 1,150 bales. Jinchang bought 1,200 bales, Zhenda 600 bales, Ruida 750 bales, Yicheng 2,500 bales, Dachangcheng 1,400 bales, Run Kang 3,900 bales, Xiecheng 1,100 bales, Hengchang 1,200 bales, Fukang 750 bales, Gengfeng 2,000 bales, Changyu 800 bales, and Shenji 800 bales. Yarn Cloth New Year Holiday for Five Days

The standard yarn flower market of the Chinese Yarn Cloth Exchange has announced that the market will be closed from December 31, 1935 to January 4, 1936 for the New Year holiday. Normal business will resume on January 5. Each broker's daily receipts and payments during the year will be settled with a 30-day period bill from December 26, it is said.

Gong He 2

The Recent Price Drops Were Too Sharp: Half of This Month's Forward Contracts Temporarily Withdrawn

Cotton Market Rebounds: Today is the last day for this month's contracts. According to market sources, merchants who had committed to deliver tens of thousands of bales at around 42 yuan per bale have withdrawn and will not deliver. Consequently, the amount of available cotton has decreased, causing the market to tighten and prices to rise again. However, spot cotton trading remains sluggish. The closing price for this month is 42.90 yuan, an increase of 1.70 yuan compared to last month.

Single Month Sees a Rise of 1.50 Yuan

Spot Cotton Market Opens: This month's trading concludes tomorrow. It's reported that some 20,000 bales were originally scheduled for delivery, but due to price declines, deliveries have been withdrawn. Simultaneously, favorable conditions in the English cotton market have boosted confidence. However, market trading is not smooth. The final spot price for this month is up 0.15 yuan from yesterday's closing price, while the forward price is down 0.10 yuan. The afternoon session opened, rising in line with the yarn market. At the same time, short sellers for this month are covering positions and not delivering, causing the price for this month to rise. Forward contracts are also doing well. The closing prices for all months in the morning session are up 0.20, 0.30, or 0.40 yuan respectively. Sales included 9,400 bales from Yuda, 1,100 bales from Zhenda, 2,900 bales from Taixing, 2,500 bales from Renfeng, 6,100 bales from Runkang, 1,600 bales from Changfeng, 2,100 bales from Dachang, 1,700 bales from Yuanxingchang, 2,400 bales from Juxing, 1,300 bales from Ruid , and 4,200 bales from Changhe. Purchases included 2,800 bales from Jifeng, 8,300 bales from Dafeng, 3,100 bales from Hexing, 2,800 bales from Wangtaixing, 2,200 bales from Minghua, 2,000 bales from Changyu, 2,100 bales from Renfeng, 2,500 bales from Tonghe, 2,000 bales from Shengyuan, 1,100 bales from Gengfeng, and 1,400 bales from Shenji. The highest and lowest prices for the day are listed below.

Slight Activity in Coarse and Fine Cotton

Spot cotton consumption is normal. Factories are not operating at full capacity. The sources include 1,800 bales from Yao Hua and 1,200 bales of Tongzhou cotton.

Strength of American Cotton Evident: Despite Large Sales, Market Prices Still Rise

Yesterday's opening of American cotton showed the strength of American cotton. Due to favorable news from Liverpool, international markets are strong. Domestic and foreign traders are buying, with prices for various months up 3 to 9 points. Later, due to profit-taking by long positions, Wall Street sold 30,000 bales of March and May contracts, causing prices to fall slightly. Half of these sales were on behalf of factories, but all were absorbed by traders. The overall trend is firm. Foreign merchants are buying distant months. Near months are softer due to large price differences. Lower-grade loan cotton may be sold. There is a lack of new entrants. The cloth market is more active. Before the close, it was reported that German and American merchants were making progress, and the public was buying, causing market prices to rise. Spot prices are up 12 points, and futures prices are up 12 to 19 points. Spot English cotton is up 1 point, and futures are up 2 to 3 points. Indian cotton exporters and futures traders are inclined to buy due to rising Japanese yarn prices. Calcutta is up or down 0.25 rupees, Oomra is up 1.25 to 1.50 rupees, and Broach is up 1 rupee. Original telegram recorded (dated 23rd).

Also, according to a telegram from Bombay, the opening forecast for the 24th is Broach at 224.5 rupees, Oomra at 204.75 rupees, and Bengal at 171.25 rupees, all up 0.75 rupees.

Grain: Barley Prices Rebound; Outside Investors Absorb Flour in Large Quantities; Market Prices Also Rebound by 6 to 7 Points Yesterday

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market, prices for various months showed signs of sharp increases. Barley prices in Chicago rebounded by 2 to 5 points, Canada rose by 4 to 5 points, and Liverpool rose by 1 pence. At the opening, this month's contract, being the last month of trading, saw selling pressure and lacked strong buying, so the trend was relatively flat. January, being the end of the lunar year, saw quieter buying, and the price increases were not very rapid. From February onwards, due to renewed strong buying from outside investors, prices rose by 3 to 6 points immediately at the opening. Trading remained active thereafter, and prices fluctuated. In the afternoon session, this month's contract opened quietly, but then continued to rise by 2 to 3 points due to customer activity. From February onwards, prices continued to rise sharply due to large purchases from outside investors, with April reaching 4.30 yuan and 2.5 cents. Later, profit-taking by traders caused prices to soften slightly. This situation is purely driven by barley prices, so prices rise or fall accordingly. The domestic market has lost its stability, it is said.

Forward Wheat Also Rises Strongly, Up More Than 10 Points; Spot Trading Has Not Started

Yesterday's forward wheat market saw strong price increases for all months in the morning session due to rebounding barley prices and continued positive sentiment. However, the price for this month was relatively stable as factories had stopped buying spot wheat. Forward contracts, on the other hand, rebounded strongly, with prices immediately rising by 8 to 10 points despite sparse trading, due to the sharp price falls of the previous day and the rebound in barley prices. In the afternoon session, trading became more active, and prices continued to stabilize, up 1 to 4 points from the morning. Spot wheat trading has still not formally started. Factories are only offering 6.55 yuan per bushel for goods from Jiangbei, while customers are holding out for 6.60 yuan, resulting in a difference of 5 points and no transactions.

Rice Market Conditions Slightly More Stable

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, shipments from various sources totaled over 100 vessels, carrying a total of 22,450 bushels of grain. Among them, thin indica rice accounted for over 40 vessels. Sales in this district were somewhat active due to the Yunnan Uprising commemoration. While wholesale trading was not brisk, the situation seemed better than before, with over 5,000 bags of thin indica rice sold. As a result, market conditions stabilized. Thick and thin japonica rice prices remained unchanged, as did Du Yang tip rice. Only Yin Yuan rice was oversupplied, resulting in a price drop of a few cents.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, 34 or 35 vessels arrived from various locations along the river. Sales of various grains in the market remained flat. However, holders of white japonica rice took advantage of the situation to sell small quantities. The morning market was quiet, but the afternoon market weakened by a few points. Early shipments were 5 to 6 points higher. Thin indica rice prices weakened again. White Yuan rice was down about 10 cents. Yangbu Du tip rice prices were flat to weak, while Ke tip rice prices held steady. Prices for other grains remained largely unchanged.

Today is the Yunnan Uprising Commemoration Day. All trading markets for rice, miscellaneous grains, flour, cotton yarn, bullion, foreign exchange, and public bonds in both the North and South are closed for the day. There will be no market reports tomorrow.

Passenger Indica Rice Oversupplied, Market Prices Fall Again by 3 to 10 Cents

Yesterday, arrivals of passenger indica rice remained high, but sales were slow. Market prices continued to weaken, falling by another 3 to 10 cents compared to the previous session. This was mainly due to the halt in passenger traffic and weak local sales. Furthermore, merchants and wholesalers were keen to sell, and Cantonese merchants had already stopped buying rice directly from Hunan Province. As Hunan rice production prices fell, supplies were bound to increase, leading to further weakness in sentiment. The overall market opened with 190 bags of Jiangxi rice, 934 bags of Hunan rice, and 1,500 bags of Han rough rice. Except for 350 bags of Xiang Jing rice, which were purchased for inland consumption, the rest was handled by this firm, it is said.

Oil Market: Soybean Oil Experiences Wild Fluctuations, Plunging 1.80 to 1.90 Yuan from Its Peak

Soybean oil prices, after rising sharply in Dalian, created an extraordinary situation. Due to a correction in Dalian, sentiment softened, and the market has been in a state of suspension for a week. Only yesterday did Dalian report a slight increase, causing prices to fall. Total trading volume included 150 lots of factory oil, 200 lots of Niuzhuang oil, 200 lots of Dalian oil, and 150 lots of Qishan oil. Prices have fallen by 1.80 to 1.90 yuan from their previous peak. Such wild fluctuations are rare in the spot market.

Securities: Last Day of the Month, Public Bonds Experience a Short Squeeze; Prices Down 60 to 70 Cents for This Month, Forward Contracts Only Down About 10 Cents

Yesterday, the public bond market at the Chinese Securities Exchange was the last day for December futures. The trend was pessimistic due to the uncertain political situation, and the short squeeze was very strong. Dealers, seeing the increasingly weak and chaotic situation, were wary, and selling and switching positions were very active. Market prices continued to fall under the stagnant surface. In the morning session, the market was quite uncertain. Major dealers such as Nos. 10, 45, etc., were mostly selling, and switching positions were very active. Nos. 51 and 11 bought a lot. Market prices fell by 10 to 45 cents. Class B and A forward contracts and Class D contracts for this month were up 5 cents. Secondary dealers were still busy switching positions, but Nos. 43 and 45 were gradually selling, and No. 50 was buying a lot. Market prices, except for Class A for this month and Class E for next month, which fell by 20 to 30 cents, were all up 5 to 35 cents. In the afternoon session, the market remained sluggish. No. 16 continued to sell or switch positions aggressively. Class C and E contracts for this month rose by 5 cents, while Class D and A contracts all fell by 10 to 45 cents. Selling pressure intensified at the close. Nos. 47, 5, 10, etc., were still selling aggressively, and retail investors were also switching positions. The short squeeze was quite intense, and prices all fell by 5 to 30 cents. Overall, prices fell by 10 to 70 cents across the board. Class B for next month was up 10 cents. The total trading volume was 12.87 million yuan. A table comparing the price increases and decreases, highs and lows is listed below (unit: yuan, trading unit: 100 yuan).

Finance: Before the Customs Closure, Bullion Prices Rise by 1.20 Yuan

Yesterday, sentiment in the gold market was better, and there was considerable buying to support prices. Sellers remained cautious, so while prices rose, trading was not very active. Early in the morning, overseas silver markets in England and America were both down. It was said that after the market closed, India would follow up and add 1.25 to the listed price, and sellers were holding back. The silver market was down 1.25. Forward silver prices in Monte Carlo were down 5 to 9.5 cents. Exchange rates fell slightly. Spot gold in London fell by 1 pence. The Central Bank's listed exchange rates showed England and America unchanged. The customs gold unit fell by 2 cents. The listed price for standard bullion fell to 1150.70 yuan. There was a lack of formal trading in the over-the-counter market. Later, with sales by German firms, the market opened slightly lower. After the opening, prices were relatively stable. Then, due to large purchases by major dealers, although the amount was small, there were not many sellers either. The HSBC's listed exchange rates showed England and America unchanged, with slight gains. Later, although the silver equalization tax fell by 2 cents, buyers continued to pour in. Lacking counterparties, prices once approached the 60 yuan mark. Then, sellers began to become active, and prices fell quickly. However, there was still support at lower levels, and the market remained stable at noon. In the afternoon session, the market was relatively stable. Later, due to a lack of supply, buyers, though not numerous, were more eager, so prices gradually rose. However, buying interest waned after the rise, and the market fluctuated.

The opening price in the morning was 1157.90 yuan, down 10 cents from the previous close. German merchants sold bars, falling back to 7.80 yuan. Fu, Yu, Yong, Ding, Kang, and Tong Taichang all bought. The HSBC's listed exchange rates showed England and America unchanged, gradually rising to 8.40 yuan. Later, although the silver equalization tax fell by 2 cents, Yuan Mao and Yong Li bought, pushing prices back up to 9.70 yuan. Retail investors and Shengyuan, Yongfu, Xingyong, Qiafeng, and Yongjingfu sold, bringing prices down to 8 yuan. Dingkang, Hengchang, Yongda, and Decheng took advantage of the lower prices to buy bars. The noon close was 1158.50 yuan.

The opening price in the afternoon session was 1158.30 yuan. Jingfu, Dingkang, Shenda, Yongda, Decheng, Qiafeng, and Yongda came in to buy, pushing prices up to 9.40 yuan. Yuanheng and Fuxingyong sold, pushing prices back down to 8.90 yuan. Chunyuanyong and others replenished slightly. The closing price was 1159.20 yuan.

The final price, based on the Central Bank's listed standard bullion price of 1150.70 yuan, was 8 yuan higher than the closing price. January was registered at 1157 yuan, and February at 1159 yuan. The replenishment price for the morning session was 1156 yuan. The spot gold price was 10 yuan higher, at 1168 yuan. The spot market was slightly weak. Refined gold was 14 yuan higher, and about 100 taels were traded between gold shops. The buying price was 19 yuan higher, and Tianjin goods were 19 yuan higher, but there were no transactions. In the switching market, Chunyuanyong sold 70 bars, and Decheng sold 35 bars, at 2.10 yuan. Yuanmaoyong sold 84 bars at 2 yuan, all of which were bought by Yicheng. The situation was cheaper in the afternoon session, which was without counterparties.

It was clear that transactions within the market were eye-catching. Overall, Dingkang, Yuanmaoyong, Hengyu, Chunyuanyong, Hengchangyong, Shendayong, etc., were on the buying side. Fuxingyong, Yongda, Decheng, Shengyuanyong, Qiafengyong, Yuanhengyong, Hongchangyong, etc., were on the selling side. Jingfu first sold and then bought. Chunyuanyong first bought and then sold.

The market was stable throughout the day. The opening price in the morning was 1157.90 yuan. The highest price was 1159.70 yuan, and the lowest price was 1157.80 yuan. The final price was 1159.20 yuan, with a range of 1.90 yuan. The result was a rebound of 1.20 yuan compared to the previous close. There were 2,527 January bar contracts, with 9 long positions and 10 short positions. There were 7,427 January/February contracts, with 34 long positions and 18 short positions. The total trading volume was 581 bars in the morning session and 84 bars in the afternoon session.

Foreign Exchange: Japanese Bank Sells Shanghai Exchange, British and American Companies Aggressively Close Shilling Positions; Interbank Trading Remains Calm

The exchange market saw some support for the Shanghai Exchange yesterday, and the result was continued stability. Early in the morning, overseas telegrams reported that London rates were down by 3.75 points for both near and far months. It was said that after the market closed, India would cover positions, adding 1.25 to the listed price, and sellers were holding back. The silver market was down 1.25. Forward silver prices in Monte Carlo were down 0.5 and 5.5 cents. Spot gold in London was down 1 pence. Sterling against US dollar was down 1.15, and Sterling against French franc was unchanged. US dollar against Sterling and US dollar against French franc were both down 0.0625. The Central Bank's listed exchange rates showed the Fire US dollar unchanged. The customs gold unit fell by 2 cents. The exchange market opened with near-term selling prices of 1 shilling, 2 pence, 4.0625 and 4.375 against each other, and US dollar at 29.53125, unchanged from the previous close for both near and far months. Banks were still buying after the opening, so while Chinese merchants were selling, the HSBC's listed exchange rates showed the Fire US dollar unchanged, and the market remained stable. Later, although the silver equalization tax fell by 2 cents, the Japanese bank slightly sold Shanghai exchange and the Dongjin Bank also sold slightly. The situation was relatively weak. However, because British and American tobacco companies aggressively closed shilling positions, the market recovered at noon. In the afternoon session, banks continued to buy far-term US dollars, with occasional trades between them. The process was difficult to change quickly. Although the Japanese bank was selling Shanghai Exchange, Chinese merchants were still buying, and the market stabilized in the end. The closing selling prices for near-term were 1 shilling, 2 pence, 4.0625 and 4.375 against each other, and US dollar at 29.53125, unchanged from the previous close. Chinese merchants slightly sold US dollars, and the Japanese bank sold Shanghai Exchange. A record of the day's transactions is listed below:
